		<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
		
	

	REQ_FORM_MODID = 'DIR';
	REQ_FORM_CATNAME = 'Engine & Engine Spare Parts';
	REQ_FORM_BGCOLOR = '#FFF0BD';
	REQ_FORM_BDR_COLOR = '#EACA93';
	REQ_FORM_LOAD_DIV_ID = 'buy_lead_gen_form';	
	REQ_FORM_TRIGGER_NAME = 'onload';	
	REQ_FORM_CAPTCHA='NO'; //for CAPTCHA Removal from this Form
	function lead_form(){
		var buylead = document.createElement('script'); buylead.type = 'text/javascript'; buylead.async = true;
		buylead.src = 'http://apps.imimg.com/blform/eto_ofr_post_form_serve.js?version=3';
		document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].appendChild(buylead);
		
	}    ;
    function open_bl_page(){
        document.getElementById('bl_overlay_layer').style.display='block';
        $('<iframe width="100%" height="100%" frameBorder="0" allowtransparency="true" scrolling="no" src="http://dir.indiamart.com/bl_overlay.html?catname=Engine %26 Engine Spare Parts">').appendTo('#bl_overlay_layer');
    }
	$(window).load(function() {
			$(this).keyup(function (e)
			{	
				if(e.keyCode === 27)
				{
						$('#bl_overlay_layer').hide();
				}
			});
			lead_form();
			//setTimeout(function(){open_bl_page()},60000);
			idleTime = 0;
			blStop = 0;
			//Increment the idle time counter every 5 minute.
			var idleInterval = setInterval(timerIncrement, 60000); // 1 minute
			
			//Zero the idle timer on mouse/keypress movement
			$(this).mousemove(function (e)
			{
				idleTime = 0;
			});
			$(this).keypress(function (e)
			{
				idleTime = 0;
			});
			function timerIncrement()
			{
				idleTime = idleTime + 1;
			if (idleTime > 4 && blStop != 1) // 5 minutes
			{
				open_bl_page();
				blStop = 1;
			}
			}
	});
	</script>
